        function doRollover(elem, rollover_color, text_color){
            // set background color of TD
            if (elem.parentNode){ // IE5, IE6 and Netscape 6
                if (rollover_color == 'transparent'){   // Netscape does not like the word "transparent".
                    elem.parentNode.bgColor = '';    
                }
                else{
                    elem.parentNode.bgColor=rollover_color;
                }
            }
            else if (elem.parentElement && elem.parentElement.setAttribute){ // IE4.
                elem.parentElement.setAttribute("bgColor", rollover_color);
            }
            else{  // Netscape 4.6x or 4.7x
                //alert("Must be Netscape! do nothing");
            }
            // set color of the link text
            if (elem.children){  // IE4, IE5, IE6 and Netscape 6
                elem.children(0).style.color=text_color;
            }
        }

                           <div><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" face="Arial" size="4"></font>&nbsp;</div>
                           <div><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" face="Arial" size="4">See article below by a Vietnam veteran who has humanitarian
                           interests in South East Asia.</font></div>
                           <div><font face="Arial"><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">The article is published on </font><a href="http://johnibii.wordpress.com/" target="_blank"><font color="black" "><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" face="Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif" color="#cc0000" size="4">Peace and Freedom II</font></font></a><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4"> </font></font></div>
                           <div><font face="Arial"><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4"></font></font>&nbsp;</div>
                           <div><font face="Arial"><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">WEBSITE:&nbsp; <font face="Arial" color="#cc0000"><a href="http://johnibii.wordpress.com/2007/08/20/vietnams-montagnards-still-under-communist-fire/" target="_blank"><font color="black" ">http://johnibii.wordpress.com/2007/08/20/vietnams-montagnards-still-under-communist-fire/</font></a></font> </font></font></div><font face="Arial">
                           </font></font><div><font face="Arial"><font face="Arial"></font></font><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" face="Arial" size="4">Regards, Scott Johnson, Advisor Montagnard Foundation.</font></div>
                           </font><div><font face="Arial"><font face="Arial"><br><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">&nbsp;</font></font></font> 
                           <div><font face="Arial"></font></div><font face="Arial"><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4"></font></font></div></div></div><font face="Arial">
                           </font><div><font face="Arial">
                           </font><div><font face="Arial"></font><a href="http://johnibii.wordpress.com/2007/08/20/vietnams-montagnards-still-under-communist-fire/" rel="bookmark" target="_blank" title="Permanent Link: Vietnam&amp;#8217;s Montagnards Still Under Communist Fire; UNHCR&amp;nbsp;Failing"><font color="black" "><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffcc" face="Impact" color="#008000" size="5">Vietnams Montagnards Still Under Communist
                              Fire; UNHCR&nbsp;Failing</font></font></a></div></div>
                           <div>
                           <div class="entry">
                           <div class="snap_preview"><font face="Arial">
                           <div id="headerimg" style="CURSOR: pointer" onclick=" location.href='http://johnibii.wordpress.com';">
                           <h1><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">August 18, 2007&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; By The Co Van</font></h1></div>
                           </font><div class="widecolumn" id="content"><font face="Arial">
                           </font><div class="post" id="post-524"><font face="Arial">
                           </font><div class="entry"><font face="Arial">
                           </font><div class="snap_preview"><font face="Arial">
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">Montagnards fleeing repression from the Central Highlands in Vietnam to
                           Cambodia have come to fear a man named Eldon that works for the UNHCR in Phnom Penh. They dont trust him and for good
                           reason. They consider him their enemy and the guy who works for the communists in Vietnam.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">Just last week, for the first time, the United Nations High Commissioner
                           on refugees in Cambodia has finally admitted that a Montagnard named Y-Phuoc Buon Krong may have been tortured in Vietnam.
                           Heres the kicker why the Montagnards can never catch a break in their human rights struggle in Vietnam. The UNHCR says
                           that they cant talk about his torture for confidentially purposes.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">I know about this type of deceit from first hand experience. I passed through
                           Phnom Penh in late 2005 and met Eldon Hagar, UNHCR field rep, and toured the Montagnard refugee camp. On every issue, Hagar
                           parroted the communist party line of the politburo in Vietnam, suspecting me to believe that besides the fabulous salary that
                           a UN worker makes, only a person ingratiating himself to the totalitarian system in Vietnam must also be a true believer.</font></p>
                           <div align="center"><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffff99" face="Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif" size="4">Email United Nations:&nbsp;
                           <a href="mailto:inquiries@un.org"><font color="black" "><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffff99" color="#cc0000">inquiries@un.org</font></font></a></font></div>
                           <div align="center"><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffff99" face="Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif" size="4">United Nations High Commissioner
                           for Refugees&nbsp; (UNHCR)<br>- CONTACT</font></div>
                           <div align="center"><a href="http://www.unhcr.org/contact.html" target="_blank"><font color="black" "><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffff99" color="#cc0000" size="4">http://www.unhcr.org/contact.html</font></font></a></div>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">The Montagnards I met in the camp told me that they were afraid to talk
                           to Eldon, because when they did, he reported what they said to the communist authorities. Then their families suffered reprisals.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">Hagar first stunned me with this silly explanation. Vietnam is no
                           longer a communist country. Its an authoritarian one, he said. That should be startling news to the Politburo
                           and the Vietnamese Communist Party that is the real power behind the Socialist Republic of Vietnam today. Perhaps Hagar doesnt
                           know about the police state control in the Provinces and Districts of Vietnam and the Peoples Party that governs at
                           every level with an iron first.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">I informed Hagar that I had just come from Vietnam where I had finally located
                           an old former South Vietnamese soldier friend of mine after 35 years. He was afraid for me to visit him in his village because
                           the police would come after I left and cause problems for him. Hagar barely listened to me. Shrugging his shoulders he said
                           that the same kind of thing happens in America. Thats strange talk for an American employed by the UNHCR.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">Hagar lectured me on what he considered the real problem in Vietnam in regard
                           to the Montagnards. The Dega Christianity (tinh lanh) practiced by the Montagnards isnt a religion at all. Its
                           a political movement led by Kok Ksor of the Montagnard Foundation in America to take back the Central Highlands. It has nothing
                           to do with religion. The Montagnards have been manipulated by outside sources.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">Eldon. Youre parroting the communist party line in Vietnam. Thats
                           the kind of stuff one reads in their newspapers controlled by the Communist Party. Its hogwash.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">But it is a fact that that Vietnamese Communist Party has confiscated huge
                           tracts of the Montagnard homeland for their own personal use. Thousands of party members were transferred south after the
                           war to take over the rich homeland and exploit the vast natural wealth there.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">Ever the apologist, Hagar has a simple excuse for that. Not only
                           did they take the Montagnard land, they took all the peasants land in Vietnam and dispersed it as they saw fit.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">My conversation with Hagar becomes more bizarre, regarding human rights
                           abuses.</font></p>
                           <div align="center"><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffff99" face="Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif" size="4">Email United Nations:&nbsp;
                           <a href="mailto:inquiries@un.org"><font color="black" "><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffff99" color="#cc0000">inquiries@un.org</font></font></a></font></div>
                           <div align="center"><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffff99" face="Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif" size="4">United Nations High Commissioner
                           for Refugees&nbsp; (UNHCR)<br>- CONTACT</font></div>
                           <div align="center"><a href="http://www.unhcr.org/contact.html" target="_blank"><font color="black" "><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffff99" color="#cc0000" size="4">http://www.unhcr.org/contact.html</font></font></a></div>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">Says Hagar, Ive been to Vietnam several times now to investigate
                           the alleged human rights abuses that the Montagnards claim happen to them. Theres nothing to it. </font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">At the time, Hagar had only been in Cambodia for 6 months and had been the
                           recipient of several carefully guided tours in Vietnam with an official escort. No one gets into the Central Highlands without
                           an official communist party minder.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">We now have an employee on our UNHCR staff that investigates the
                           reported human rights abuses. He is a Vietnamese based in Hanoi, Hagar proudly boasts.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">Do you really believe that the communist party power apparatus would
                           allow a Vietnamese to conduct an independent investigation?  I asked.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">Hagars next statement epitomizes the sell out of the Montagnards
                           by the UNHCR when he answered, Yes, by all means. Why wouldnt we trust his reports? He wouldnt jeopardize
                           his job with us to report falsely. And if there were really any human rights abuses, dont you think the American CIA
                           would know about them? Dont you think they have spies in the Central Highlands?</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">The UNHCR rep in Hanoi is Vu Anh Son. Following a field trip to the Central
                           Highlands in Oct 5-6 of 05, he came back with a glowing report. He stated that 8 of the 13 returned Montagnards are leading
                           good lives with high stable incomes. Each of the target families earns up to hundreds of millions of Vietnamese dong a year
                           (equal to approximately 6000 dollars)</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">For UNHCR to accept such a report is ludicrous and just plain dumb on their
                           part to make it public. The $6000 a year is 30 times what a peasant in Vietnam can make in a year. Some of the best factory
                           jobs around Saigon pay 100 dollars a month. The proselytizing department in Hanoi that directs the UNHCR rep behind the scenes
                           needs to learn how to write more credible propaganda reports.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">No one with an ounce of sense about the situation on the ground in Vietnam
                           would believe such nonsense. Its written for those living in the extended age of childhood, or could the UNHCR and
                           Hagar be that nave? Do they know how stupid they look by parroting such nonsense?</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">After spending several hours with Hagar, its plain to see why none
                           of the human rights organizations in Phnom Penh have any respect for UNHCR. They have compromised themselves by trying to
                           appease the tyrants who are committing what many human rights organization say is genocide against the Montagnards in Vietnam.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">In July of 05, one hundred Montagnards under the care of the UNHCR were
                           forced back to Vietnam. The guards employed night sticks and electric batons on the Montagnards who sat on the ground and
                           refused to get on the buses to transport them back to Vietnam. Eighteen NGOs in Phnom Penh signed a letter of protest
                           to the Cambodian government over the abuse. I even talked to a human rights worker who witnessed the event.</font></p>
                           <div align="center"><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffff99" face="Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif" size="4">Email United Nations:&nbsp;
                           <a href="mailto:inquiries@un.org"><font color="black" "><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffff99" color="#cc0000">inquiries@un.org</font></font></a></font></div>
                           <div align="center"><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffff99" face="Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif" size="4">United Nations High Commissioner
                           for Refugees&nbsp; (UNHCR)<br>- CONTACT</font></div>
                           <div align="center"><a href="http://www.unhcr.org/contact.html" target="_blank"><font color="black" "><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffff99" color="#cc0000" size="4">http://www.unhcr.org/contact.html</font></font></a></div>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">View also this interview-</font></p>
                           <p><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=IOSKDjYPyXU" target="_blank"><font color="black" "><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" color="#b85b5a" size="4">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=IOSKDjYPyXU</font></font></a><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">&nbsp;</font></p>
                           <p><br><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">you can listen to a Montagnard refugee who escaped to the US testify
                           how he witnessed Eldon authorize the forced return and brutal beatings of these 100 Montagnard men, woman and
                           children.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">But Hagar offers another alibi. Their source of information is a
                           Human Rights Watch representative here in Phnom Penh. Human Rights Watch is not a credible source of truth here.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">HAGAR and the UNHCR are quite willing to accept anything the police state
                           of Vietnam tells them, and to deny the legitimate humans rights abuses that the Montagnards have suffered for 32 years since
                           the end of the Vietnam War.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">Montagnards today are still fleeing Vietnam into the two eastern Provinces
                           of Cambodia where they are hunted down for bounties and sold back to the Vietnamese Police authorities. The UNHCRs
                           response to this was to move their refugee camp from the Vietnamese/Cambodia border back to Phnom Penh, a distance of 200
                           kilometers-an impossible distance for a fleeing Montagnard to reach safety.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">Russian writer Alexander Solzhenitsyn, a long-time prisoner in the Communist
                           Gulag, would have this to say to Hagar about the UNHCRs unchallenged acceptance of what the police state system feeds
                           them from Hanoi. During my time in the camps, I had got to know the enemies of the human race quite well. They respect
                           the big fist and nothing else. The harder you slug them, the safer you will be.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">Unlike Solzhenitsyn, it seems that Eldon Hagar and the UNHCR officials in
                           Phnom Penh have become appeasers and a doormat to the enemies of the human race.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">Now, you will have to decide who is telling the truth here in Phnom
                           Penh, said Hagar as I left.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">The NGO community has their own agenda, but we at UNHCR dont
                           have one. Were here to help the Montagnards.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">That parting line could not have been scripted better by beloved Big Brother
                           in Hanoi, Vu Anh Son, who is also there to help the Montagnards.</font></p>
                           <p><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">The Co Van<br>Southeast Asian Traveler and Vietnam Veteran<br>Aug 2007</font></p>
                           <div align="center"><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffff99" face="Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif" size="4">Email United Nations:&nbsp;
                           <a href="mailto:inquiries@un.org"><font color="black" "><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffff99" color="#cc0000">inquiries@un.org</font></font></a></font></div>
                           <div align="center"><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffff99" face="Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif" size="4">United Nations High Commissioner
                           for Refugees&nbsp; (UNHCR)<br>- CONTACT</font></div>
                           <div align="center"><a href="http://www.unhcr.org/contact.html" target="_blank"><font color="black" "><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffff99" color="#cc0000" size="4">http://www.unhcr.org/contact.html</font></font></a></div>
                           <div align="center">&nbsp;</div>
                           </font><p><font face="Arial"><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffff99" size="4">For more information, go to the <strong>Montagnard Foundation</strong>:<br></font><a href="http://www.montagnard-foundation.org/homepage.html" target="_blank"><font color="black" "><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffff99" color="#cc0000" size="4">http://www.montagnard-foundation.org/homepage.html</font></font></a></font><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff" size="4">&nbsp;</font></p>
                           <p><font size="4"></font>&nbsp;</p>
